TeamProject2 Part2

Quarto

Quarto enables you to weave together content and executable code into a finished document. To learn more about Quarto see https://quarto.org.

Running Code

When you click the Render button a document will be generated that includes both content and the output of embedded code. You can embed code like this:

# Install packages

Read Files

seg<- read.csv("C:/Users/liua8/Desktop/customer analysis/TP_CAdata.csv", header=TRUE)

Standardize Necessary Variables that Related to Consumers’ Needs

# Select relevant columns and standardize the data
standardized_seg <- seg[,-1] %>% select(AtmosImp, AvgCost, LunchFreq, DinnerFreq, FoodImp, ServImp, NumInParty)

# Check the structure or summary of the standardized data
summary(standardized_seg)

ca_data_scaled <- scale(standardized_seg)

Run Analysis with 5 clusters

 # Run k-means with 6 segments
# Convert the scaled data back to a data frame
ca_data_scaled_df <- as.data.frame(ca_data_scaled)

# Run k-means with 5 segments
seg_kmeans <- kmeans(x = ca_data_scaled_df[, c("AtmosImp", "LunchFreq", "FoodImp", "AvgCost", "DinnerFreq", "ServImp", "NumInParty")], centers = 5)
scaled_data <- ca_data_scaled
# Compute the Euclidean distance matrix
distance_matrix <- dist(scaled_data, method = "euclidean")

# Perform hierarchical clustering using the complete linkage method
seg_hclust <- hclust(distance_matrix, method = "complete")
plot(seg_hclust)

Silhouette Score with 5 Clusters

library(stats)
library(cluster)
Warning: package 'cluster' was built under R version 4.4.2
library(factoextra)
Warning: package 'factoextra' was built under R version 4.4.2
Loading required package: ggplot2
Welcome! Want to learn more? See two factoextra-related books at https://goo.gl/ve3WBa
# Assuming ca_data_scaled is already a scaled dataset
scaled_data <- as.data.frame(ca_data_scaled)  # Ensure it's a data frame

# Run k-means clustering with 5 segments
seg_kmeans <- kmeans(scaled_data[, c("AtmosImp", "LunchFreq", "FoodImp", "AvgCost", "DinnerFreq", "ServImp", "NumInParty")], 
                      centers = 5, nstart = 25)

# Compute the Euclidean distance matrix for hierarchical clustering
distance_matrix <- dist(scaled_data, method = "euclidean")

# Perform hierarchical clustering using complete linkage
seg_hclust <- hclust(distance_matrix, method = "complete")

# Plot dendrogram
plot(seg_hclust, main = "Dendrogram of Hierarchical Clustering", sub = "", xlab = "")

# Add rectangles to the dendrogram to show the clusters
rect.hclust(seg_hclust, k = 5, border = 2:6)
# Determine the number of clusters (e.g., k = 5)
k <- 5
cluster_assignments <- cutree(seg_hclust, k = k)

# Compute silhouette scores
silhouette_score <- silhouette(cluster_assignments, distance_matrix)

# Print silhouette summary
summary(silhouette_score)

Run Analysis with 6 Clusters - Silhouette Score

# Load required libraries
library(stats)
library(cluster)
library(factoextra)

# Assuming ca_data_scaled is already a scaled dataset
scaled_data <- as.data.frame(ca_data_scaled)  # Ensure it's a data frame

# Run k-means clustering with 6 segments
seg_kmeans <- kmeans(scaled_data[, c("AtmosImp", "LunchFreq", "FoodImp", "AvgCost", "DinnerFreq", "ServImp", "NumInParty")], 
                      centers = 6, nstart = 36)

# Compute the Euclidean distance matrix for hierarchical clustering
distance_matrix <- dist(scaled_data, method = "euclidean")

# Perform hierarchical clustering using complete linkage
seg_hclust <- hclust(distance_matrix, method = "complete")

# Plot dendrogram
plot(seg_hclust, main = "Dendrogram of Hierarchical Clustering", sub = "", xlab = "")

# Add rectangles to the dendrogram to show the clusters
rect.hclust(seg_hclust, k = 6, border = 2:6)
# Determine the number of clusters (e.g., k = 5)
k <- 6
cluster_assignments <- cutree(seg_hclust, k = k)

# Compute silhouette scores
silhouette_score <- silhouette(cluster_assignments, distance_matrix)

# Print silhouette summary
summary(silhouette_score)
Silhouette of 200 units in 6 clusters from silhouette.default(x = cluster_assignments, dist = distance_matrix) :

Individual silhouette widths:
   Min. 1st Qu.  Median    Mean 3rd Qu.    Max. 
 0.2546  0.5534  0.6290  0.6181  0.6963  0.7751 
# Visualize silhouette plot
fviz_silhouette(silhouette_score)

Elbow Chart

# Elbow plot for first 10 segments
x <- c(1:10)
sort_height <- sort(seg_hclust$height,decreasing=TRUE)
y <- sort_height[1:10]
plot(x,y); lines(x,y,col="blue")

Calculate Number of Consumers in Each Cluster

clusters_hclust <- cutree(seg_hclust, k = 6)

# Count the number of people in each cluster
cluster_counts_hclust <- table(clusters_hclust)
print(cluster_counts_hclust)

Profiling Consumers Based on General Characteristics

Standardize Data

# Select relevant columns and standardize the data
profile_seg <- seg[,-1] %>% select(Gender, Race,Tvfreq,Webfreq,OOHfreq, Radiofreq, Smfreq,HHI, NumKids, Age)

# Check the structure or summary of the standardized data
summary(profile_seg)

# Scale the numeric columns
numeric_columns <- profile_seg %>% select(Tvfreq, Webfreq, OOHfreq, Radiofreq, Smfreq, HHI, NumKids, Age)
scaled_numeric_columns <- scale(numeric_columns)

# Combine the scaled numeric columns with the unscaled Gender and Race columns
profile_data_scaled <- cbind(profile_seg %>% select(Gender, Race), scaled_numeric_columns)

Add column “Cluster”

# Convert to data frame
profile_data_scaled <- as.data.frame(profile_data_scaled)
profile_data_scaled$Cluster <- clusters_hclust
profile_data_scaled$Gender <- ifelse(profile_data_scaled$Gender == 1, "Male", "Female")

Analysis on Clustering Consumers Based on General Characteristics

# Convert to data frame
ca_data_scaled <- as.data.frame(ca_data_scaled)
ca_data_scaled$Cluster <- clusters_hclust
library(dplyr)

profile_summary <- profile_data_scaled %>%
  group_by(Cluster) %>%
  summarise(
    Avg_Age = mean(Age, na.rm = TRUE),
    Gender_Distribution = paste0(round(mean(Gender == "Male", na.rm = TRUE) * 100, 1), "% Male"),
    Avg_Income = mean(HHI, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_TV_Hours = mean(Tvfreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_WEB = mean(Webfreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_Out_of_Home_ads = mean(OOHfreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_Radio_freq = mean(Radiofreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_social_media_freq = mean(Smfreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_Numkids = mean(NumKids, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_race = mean(Race, na.rm = TRUE)
  )

print(profile_summary)

Profiling Based on selected variables that are relevant to Restaurant

library(dplyr)

# Convert to data frame
ca_data_scaled <- as.data.frame(ca_data_scaled)

# Group by Cluster and summarize
profile_summary_restaurant <- ca_data_scaled %>%
  group_by(Cluster) %>%
  summarise(
    Avg_Atoms_Imp = mean(AtmosImp, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_Cost = mean(AvgCost, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_LunchFreq = mean(LunchFreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_DinnerFreq = mean(DinnerFreq, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_FoodImp = mean(FoodImp, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_ServIMP = mean(ServImp, na.rm = TRUE),
    Avg_NumInParty = mean(NumInParty, na.rm = TRUE)
  )

print(profile_summary_restaurant)
